[30;1m85 | [0m[35mand automatically modifies the appropriate ``RPATH`` entries such that these libraries[0m

[30;1m88 | [0m[35madvised that bundling, like static linking, may implicate copyright concerns.[0m

[30;1m34 | [0m[35m``auditwheel repair``: copies these external shared libraries into the wheel itself,[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35mand automatically modifies the appropriate ``RPATH`` entries such that these libraries[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35mwill be picked up at runtime. This accomplishes a similar result as if the libraries had[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35mbeen statically linked without requiring changes to the build system. Packagers are[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35madvised that bundling, like static linking, may implicate copyright concerns.[0m
